title: Tech_Teams_by_Country_1.1

::: mw-parser-output
This is a list of all tech teams for each country as of HoI 2 version
1.1. The order of columns is: Team #, Team Name, Picture #, Skill, Start
Year, End Year, Specialties. The specialty abbreviations are listed at
the bottom of this document.
